\documentclass[11pt]{article}

    
    
    \usepackage[T1]{fontenc}

    % Basic figure setup, for now with no caption control since it's done
    % automatically by Pandoc (which extracts ![](path) syntax from Markdown).
    \usepackage{graphicx}
    % We will generate all images so they have a width \maxwidth. This means
    % that they will get their normal width if they fit onto the page, but
    % are scaled down if they would overflow the margins.
    \makeatletter
    \def\maxwidth{\ifdim\Gin@nat@width>\linewidth\linewidth
    \else\Gin@nat@width\fi}
    \makeatother
    \let\Oldincludegraphics\includegraphics
    % Set max figure width to be 80% of text width, for now hardcoded.
    \renewcommand{\includegraphics}[1]{\Oldincludegraphics[width=.8\maxwidth]{#1}}
    % Ensure that by default, figures have no caption (until we provide a
    % proper Figure object with a Caption API and a way to capture that
    % in the conversion process - todo).
    \usepackage{caption}
    \DeclareCaptionLabelFormat{nolabel}{}
    \captionsetup{labelformat=nolabel}

    \usepackage{adjustbox} % Used to constrain images to a maximum size 
    \usepackage{xcolor} % Allow colors to be defined
    \usepackage{enumerate} % Needed for markdown enumerations to work
    \usepackage{geometry} % Used to adjust the document margins
    \usepackage{amsmath} % Equations
    \usepackage{amssymb} % Equations
    \usepackage{textcomp} % defines textquotesingle
    % Hack from http://tex.stackexchange.com/a/47451/13684:
    \AtBeginDocument{%
        \def\PYZsq{\textquotesingle}% Upright quotes in Pygmentized code
    }
    \usepackage{upquote} % Upright quotes for verbatim code
    \usepackage{eurosym} % defines \euro
    \usepackage[mathletters]{ucs} % Extended unicode (utf-8) support
    \usepackage[utf8x]{inputenc} % Allow utf-8 characters in the tex document
    \usepackage{fancyvrb} % verbatim replacement that allows latex
    \usepackage{grffile} % extends the file name processing of package graphics

    \usepackage[normalem]{ulem} % ulem is needed to support strikethroughs (\sout)

             \PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:}
                 \PY{n}{graph}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{secondColumn}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{firstColumn}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}
             
             
             \PY{l+s+sd}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}Implementation of Shortest Path Function        }
         \PY{l+s+sd}{    \PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}    
         \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{findShortestPath}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{graph}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{source}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
             \PY{n}{visited}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}                  
             \PY{n}{level}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}               
             \PY{n}{nextlevel}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{source}\PY{p}{:}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}  
             \PY{k}{while} \PY{n}{nextlevel}\PY{p}{:}
                 \PY{n}{actuallevel}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{nextlevel}  
                 \PY{n}{nextlevel}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}         
                 \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{v} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{actuallevel}\PY{p}{:}
                     \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{v} \PY{o+ow}{not} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{visited}\PY{p}{:}
                         \PY{n}{visited}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{v}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{level} 
                         \PY{n}{nextlevel}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{update}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{graph}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{v}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)} 
                 \PY{n}{level}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{level}\PY{o}{+}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}
             \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{visited}  
         
                 
             \PY{l+s+sd}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}Implementation of Closeness Centrality Function  }
         \PY{l+s+sd}{    \PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}
         \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{ClosenessCentralityFunction}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{Graf}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{u}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{None}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
             \PY{n}{closeness\PYZus{}centrality} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}
             \PY{n}{vertex} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
             \PY{n}{i} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}
             \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{key}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{value} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{Graf}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{items}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                 \PY{n}{vertex}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{key}\PY{p}{)}
             
             \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{n} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{vertex}\PY{p}{:}
                 \PY{n}{dictShortestPath} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{findShortestPath}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{Graf}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{n}\PY{p}{)}
                 \PY{n}{totalPath} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{sum}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{dictShortestPath}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{values}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
                 \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{totalPath} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.0} \PY{o+ow}{and} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{Graf}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{:}
                     \PY{n}{closeness\PYZus{}centrality}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{n}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{dictShortestPath}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mf}{1.0}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n}{totalPath}
                     \PY{n}{s} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{dictShortestPath}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mf}{1.0}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{p}{(} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{Graf}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{p}{)}
                     \PY{n}{closeness\PYZus{}centrality}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{n}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{*}\PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{s}
                 \PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:}
                     \PY{n}{closeness\PYZus{}centrality}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{n}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.0}
             \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{u} \PY{o+ow}{is} \PY{o+ow}{not} \PY{k+kc}{None}\PY{p}{:}
                 \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{closeness\PYZus{}centrality}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{u}\PY{p}{]}
             \PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:}
                 \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{closeness\PYZus{}centrality}
         
         \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{top25pages}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{scores}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
             \PY{l+s+sd}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}

             \PY{n}{table} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{sorted}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{scores}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{items}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{key} \PY{o}{=} \PY{k}{lambda} \PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{reverse} \PY{o}{=} \PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{)}
             \PY{n}{headers} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Pages}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Closeness Centrality Scores}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}
             \PY{n+nb}{print} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{tb}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{tabulate}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{table}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{:}\PY{l+m+mi}{25}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{headers}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{tablefmt} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{rst}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

                 \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{graph} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{graph}

         \PY{l+s+sd}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}
         \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{computePageRank}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{graph}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{damping\PYZus{}factor} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.80}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{eps} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.00001}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
             \PY{n}{vertices} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{graph}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{vertices}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}    
             \PY{n}{old\PYZus{}prank}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{new\PYZus{}prank} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}
             \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{vertex} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{graph}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{vertices}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                 \PY{n}{old\PYZus{}prank}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{vertex}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mf}{1.0}\PY{o}{/}\PY{n}{vertices}
             \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{iter\PYZus{}} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{range}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{101}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                 \PY{n+nb}{print} \PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Iteration: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZpc{}d}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}} \PY{o}{\PYZpc{}} \PY{n}{iter\PYZus{}}\PY{p}{)}        
                 \PY{n}{diff} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
                 \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{u} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{graph}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{vertices}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                     \PY{n}{rank} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{n}{damping\PYZus{}factor}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{/}\PY{n}{vertices}
                     \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{v} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{graph}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{vertices}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                         \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{u} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{graph}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{getGraph}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{v}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{:}
                             \PY{n}{rank} \PY{o}{+}\PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{damping\PYZus{}factor}\PY{o}{*}\PY{n}{old\PYZus{}prank}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{v}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{/}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{graph}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{getGraph}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{v}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
                     \PY{n}{diff}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{abs}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{old\PYZus{}prank}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{u}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{rank}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
                     \PY{n}{new\PYZus{}prank}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{u}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{rank}
                 \PY{n}{old\PYZus{}prank} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{copy}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{deepcopy}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{new\PYZus{}prank}\PY{p}{)}
                 \PY{n}{new\PYZus{}prank}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{clear}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
                 \PY{k}{if} \PY{n+nb}{sum}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{diff}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{n}{eps}\PY{p}{:}
                     \PY{n+nb}{print} \PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Total iterations: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZpc{}d}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}} \PY{o}{\PYZpc{}} \PY{n}{iter\PYZus{}}\PY{p}{)}
                     \PY{k}{break}
             \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{old\PYZus{}prank}
         
         \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{top25pages}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{scores}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
             \PY{l+s+sd}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}
         \PY{l+s+sd}{    Display the top 25 users in the graph ranked by}
         \PY{l+s+sd}{    their page rank scores}
         \PY{l+s+sd}{    \PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}
             \PY{n}{table} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{sorted}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{scores}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{items}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{key} \PY{o}{=} \PY{k}{lambda} \PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{reverse} \PY{o}{=} \PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{)}
             \PY{n}{headers} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Pages}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Page\PYZhy{}Rank Scores}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}
             \PY{n+nb}{print} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{tb}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{tabulate}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{table}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{:}\PY{l+m+mi}{25}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{headers}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{tablefmt} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{rst}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
